### [162] [Predicting Mergeability of Parameter-Efficient Fine-Tuning Updates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19549)
*Lin Tang,Wei Zhang,Jing Li,Hongyu Chen,Ming Zhao,Yuxuan Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 MergeProbe，通过分析训练初期的指标，能在合并 LoRA 适配器前预测其兼容性，从而在避免破坏性干扰的同时降低部署成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 LoRA 适配器合并通常在训练完成后才进行，缺乏对合并后性能的预见性，导致强独立性能的适配器在合并时可能产生破坏性干扰，造成巨大的计算和时间成本浪费。

Method: 提出了 MergeProbe 方法，通过分析训练初期的低秩更新及梯度在各任务间的对齐程度，以及对共享表示的扰动程度，来预测适配器（adapter）的可合并性。该方法利用这些信号实现对合并策略（直接合并、重加权、剪枝或路由）的自动化决策。

Result: 在包含数学、代码、科学、指令遵循和安全五个领域的 MERGE-PEFT 基准测试中，MergeProbe 在保持适配器任务效用方面表现最优（平均和最差情况性能提升），且相比全任务路由方案显著降低了部署开销。

Conclusion: LoRA 模型合并不再是一个单纯的事后工程步骤，而可以转化为一个可预测的度量问题。MergeProbe 能够有效地在训练早期预测合并性能，为高效的 PEFT 模型组合提供了稳健的决策依据。

Abstract: Low-rank adaptation (LoRA) makes it cheap to train many domain- and task-specific language model adapters, but whether two adapters can be merged is usually discovered only after both have been fully trained and evaluated. This late feedback is costly: adapters that are strong in isolation can interfere destructively once their updates are combined. We ask whether this outcome can be anticipated. We formalize adapter mergeability as the degree to which an adapter preserves its single-task utility after merging, and show that it can be forecast from signals measured in the first few percent of training -- chiefly how the low-rank updates and their gradients align across tasks and how much they disturb shared representations. We package these signals into MergeProbe, a lightweight predictor that estimates pairwise and set-level retention and turns the estimate into a concrete decision: merge directly, reweight, prune, or route. On MERGE-PEFT, a five-domain benchmark spanning math, code, science, instruction following, and safety, MergeProbe attains the best average and worst-case retention among strong interference-aware merge baselines while adding far less deployment overhead than full task routing. This turns LoRA merging from a post-hoc engineering step into an anticipatory measurement problem.

### [163] [Displacement Is Not Direction: Evaluating Fidelity Metrics for Quantized LLM Deployment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19558)
*Miloš Nikolić,Ali Hadi Zadeh,Enrique Torres Sanchez,Andreas Moshovos*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究发现KL散度等保真度指标虽常用于量化模型评估，但在模型性能接近基准的区域完全失效，且无法有效预测具体任务的执行成功率，不应作为衡量量化模型质量的可靠代理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量化模型评估通常使用KL散度等保真度指标作为基准测试的低成本代理。本文旨在质疑这种做法的有效性，探讨这些指标是否能准确反映量化模型在实际任务中的真实性能表现。

Method: 研究人员选取了两个大规模量化模型群组（Qwen3.6-35B-A3B和Devstral-Small-2-24B），通过测试14种不同的保真度测量变体（包括KL散度、困惑度、Top-1一致性等），在多个下游基准测试上进行相关性分析。同时，通过分析LiveCodeBench上的失败预测能力和跨模型路由准确性，从结构分解的角度揭示了保真度指标与基准性能之间关系的失效原因。

Result: 实验发现，尽管KL散度在全量程内与基准得分呈强相关（相关系数ρ分别为-0.72和-0.86），但在性能接近基准的“静默区”内，相关性降为非显著；在预测具体任务失败时表现较弱，且作为跨模型路由器的准确率仅为42.3%至49.4%，表现不及随机水平。研究证实了保真度指标在精细评估中的失效。

Conclusion: 基于KL散度等保真度指标来评估大模型量化效果存在局限性。虽然这些指标在量化程度较深时（全局范围内）表现出较强的相关性，但在模型性能接近基准的“静默区”内会完全失效。此外，该指标在预测单个提示词失败及作为跨模型路由器的能力上表现不佳，研究认为这是因为KL散度主要反映了与参考模型的不一致程度（量），而非不一致的性质（质）。

Abstract: Fidelity metrics, such as per-token KL divergence (KLD) against a high-precision reference, are often used in practice as low-cost proxies for benchmark quality. We test this practice on a 28-quant cohort of Qwen3.6-35B-A3B and a 41-quant cohort of Devstral-Small-2-24B, evaluated across a suite of downstream benchmarks. We find that KLD is strongly correlated with benchmark score over the full cohort ($ρ=-0.72$ on Qwen and $ρ=-0.86$ on Devstral, both with $p<0.001$). However, this relationship collapses to non-significance in the near-baseline silent zone ($ρ=+0.00$ on Qwen and $ρ=-0.24$, $p=0.36$, on Devstral). This collapse persists across 14 measurement variants, including different KLD aggregations, perplexity formulations, top-1 agreement, calibration corpora, and context lengths. At the per-prompt level, KLD has only weak failure-prediction power on code, with failed-vs-passed geometric-mean ratios in $[1.08,1.22]$ across five models on LiveCodeBench, and fails as a cross-model router, achieving only $42.3\%-49.4\%$ accuracy on disagreement prompts. We trace the collapse to a structural decomposition: KLD primarily measures the volume of disagreement with the reference, with silent-zone composite $ρ=+0.94$ ($p<0.001$) on Qwen and $+0.55$ ($p=0.03$) on Devstral, while its relationship to the direction of those disagreements is weak and task-conditional.

</details>


### [164] [Understanding Key Features of Time Series Foundation Models from Epidemic Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19560)
*Alireza Jafari,Judy Fox,Geoffrey C. Fox,Madhav Marathe,Aniruddha Adiga*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究系统评估了多种现代机器学习模型在区域流感短期预测中的表现，发现融合多种预训练模型的“专家混合架构”性能最优，证明了异构预训练特征的互补价值，并指出数值型Transformer比LLM更适合此类时间序列预测任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 季节性流感每年造成巨大的公共卫生负担，准确的短期预测对于疫苗接种安排、医院人力配置及资源调配至关重要。目前学术界对现代预测架构在传染病监测数据上的比较研究尚不充分，缺乏系统性的评估以指导实际应用中的模型选择和预训练策略。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过结合多种预训练预测器的“专家混合模型（MoE）”是流感预测的最佳方案，异构预训练表示能够提供互补信息。数值型Transformer模型表现稳健，且预训练在长视距预测中增益最大，尤其是当预训练领域与流感动力学机制相关时。相比之下，基于LLM的时间序列模型在该场景下表现欠佳。此外，将住院数据作为辅助变量能有效增强多视距预测的稳健性。

Abstract: Seasonal influenza infects millions of people and causes substantial morbidity and mortality in the United States each year, making accurate short-term forecasting a core public-health need. Reliable forecasts of epidemic time series can inform vaccination timing, hospital staffing, and resource allocation, yet the comparative behavior of modern forecasting architectures on infectious-disease surveillance data remains insufficiently characterized. We address this gap through a systematic evaluation of regional influenza forecasting using influenza-like illness surveillance and influenza-associated hospitalization time series under both temporal and spatial generalization settings for 1-4-week-ahead prediction. We compare classical neural network architectures, numerical transformer-based models, pretrained time series foundation models, and LLM-based forecasting approaches. Across tasks, we demonstrate that a mixture-of-experts model that fuses multiple pretrained forecasters achieves the strongest overall performance, indicating that heterogeneous pretrained representations provide complementary predictive information. Our results further show that numerical transformer-based models produce reliable forecasts, while pretraining provides the largest gains at longer horizons, particularly when the pretraining domain is mechanistically aligned with influenza dynamics. In contrast, LLM-based time series methods underperform relative to numerical forecasters in this setting. Finally, we examine hospitalization information as both an auxiliary covariate and a pretraining source. Hospitalization signals provide complementary improvements in selected settings and clarify when additional surveillance streams enhance the robustness of multi-horizon forecasting. These findings provide actionable guidance on model selection, pretraining strategy, and auxiliary-signal use for influenza preparedness.

### [165] [Advances in Scientific Machine Learning for Coupled Fluid Flow and Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19562)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 科学机器学习（SciML）为处理复杂的耦合流体流动与传输问题提供了一种高效的替代方案，能在保持较高准确性的前提下显著降低计算成本。尽管目前在实时预测和不确定性量化方面仍存在挑战，但该领域的技术正在快速演进，为复杂物理系统的快速模拟奠定了基础。

Abstract: This chapter reviews recent advances in Scientific Machine Learning (SciML) for modeling coupled fluid flow and transport phenomena governed by the incompressible Navier-Stokes and scalar transport equations. Such systems, found in applications like turbidity currents and thermal convection, feature strong nonlinear coupling and multiscale behavior that make high-fidelity simulations computationally expensive. To address this, the chapter surveys state-of-the-art SciML methods for building efficient surrogate models, including linear reduced-order techniques based on Singular Value Decomposition (such as Dynamic Mode Decomposition) and nonlinear neural network approaches like Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs) and $β$-Variational Autoencoders ($β$-VAEs). It first covers the authors' work combining these models with High Performance Computing strategies, including Adaptive Mesh Refinement/Coarsening (AMR/C) and scientific floating-point data compression. It then presents two new contributions: surrogate modeling of turbidity currents via PINNs, and the extraction of disentangled nonlinear modes from thermal flows using $β$-VAEs. Governing equations and representative benchmarks, including lock-exchange flows and Rayleigh-Bénard convection, illustrate these methodologies. The chapter is intentionally long, covering both the mathematical and physical foundations of coupled fluid flow and the computational aspects of state-of-the-art modeling. Overall, it demonstrates how SciML enables fast, accurate approximations of complex coupled systems within the specific data regimes and modeling assumptions considered, while substantially reducing computational cost relative to full-order simulations. Broader capabilities such as real-time prediction and uncertainty quantification remain active research directions whose feasibility depends strongly on the problem at hand.

### [166] [On the QUEST for Uncertainty Quantification via Highest Density Regions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19569)
*Sam Goring,Tom Kuipers,Nicola Paoletti,David S. Watson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对回归问题中传统不确定性量化方法存在的不足，本文提出了QUEST框架，通过最高密度区域体积来衡量不确定性，在理论公理化和实际性能上均优于现有的评分规则方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的回归问题标量不确定性量化方法（如基于恰当评分规则的方法）在目标统计量并非条件期望时，往往会产生违反直觉的结果，无法准确表征不确定性。

Method: 提出了一种名为QUEST（Quantifying Uncertainty via highest dEnSiTy regions）的框架，该框架基于分布支撑集中在峰值处的勒贝格测度（Lebesgue measure），通过一个或多个鲁棒性参数α来评估不确定性，并与信息论及经济学中的经典统计量建立了联系。

Result: QUEST满足不确定性量化文献中的多项公理（如分布扩展下的单调性和位置平移不变性），在选择性预测基准测试中，QUEST在性能上优于方差和微分熵等标准度量。

Conclusion: QUEST通过基于最高密度区域的测度，为回归问题提供了一种更符合直觉、更具理论严谨性的不确定性量化方法，能够更好地表征认知不确定性和偶然不确定性。

Abstract: Uncertainty quantification (UQ) is essential for reliable decision-making in safety-critical applications in probabilistic machine learning. For regression problems, dominant scalar UQ approaches - notably, those based on proper scoring rules - measure uncertainty via pointwise predictive risk. This can lead to counterintuitive results when the target statistic is not the conditional expectation. We propose an alternative framework, in which uncertainty is characterised by the volume of the most probable subset of a distribution's support. QUEST (Quantifying Uncertainty via highest dEnSiTy regions) is a novel approach to UQ based on the concentration of Lebesgue measure at a distribution's peak(s), evaluated at one or more values of a robustness parameter $α$. We establish connections between our measures and classical statistics from information theory and economics. We show that, unlike popular alternatives based on proper scoring rules, QUEST measures of epistemic and aleatoric uncertainty satisfy a set of axioms adapted from the UQ literature, including monotonicity under distributional spread and invariance to location shifts. Selective prediction benchmarks confirm that QUEST performs favourably against standard measures such as variance and differential entropy.

Abstract: Causal abstractions formalize when a high-level structural causal model (SCM) captures the interventional behavior of a lower-level SCM. Existing applications of this notion largely follow a hypothesis-testing paradigm: an expert proposes a candidate high-level model and then evaluates if the low-level system implements it. We study the complementary problem of learning a high-level model directly from low-level measurements. Our contributions leverage hypotheses from low-rank causal discovery, and can be summarized as follows: (1) we show that observations generated by a low-rank graph induce latents that form a causal abstraction, (2) we provide identifiability results about these latents, and (3) we propose a practical objective to learn this high-level SCM.

Does it avoid re-delivering content the user already heard?
  We introduce IHBench (Interruption Handling Benchmark), a benchmark that evaluates post-interruption recovery in voice agents executing state-machine-driven workflows across 10 enterprise domains. Six interruption types are injected at controlled points mid-utterance, with per-interruption evaluation rubrics generated alongside the data.   We evaluate 27 audio-language model configurations from OpenAI, Google, and the open-weight community. Models vary widely, and recovery quality depends strongly on the interruption type. Across our experiments, closed-weight models are consistently more robust to interruptions than open-weight ones: they win far more often on task fulfillment, degrade roughly 3.3x more slowly as conversations grow longer, and show no audio-versus-text modality gap, whereas the open-weight models lose ground on all three. ### [169] [Comparing Linear Probes with Mahalanobis Cosine Similarity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19603)
*Zhuofan Josh Ying,Peter Hase,Nikolaus Kriegeskorte*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究证明了马氏余弦相似度（MCS）是评估线性探测器分布外（OOD）性能的优越指标，并从理论上揭示了其与 OOD AUROC 之间线性相关性的数学本质，为可解释性研究中的模型评估提供了理论支撑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 线性探测器常用于可解释性研究，但通常使用的欧氏余弦相似度缺乏足够的任务感知能力。先前研究发现马氏余弦相似度（MCS）能极好地预测分布外（OOD）性能，本研究旨在验证该现象的普适性，并从理论上推导其成因及边界条件。

Method: 研究人员通过跨模型、层级和概念领域的实证分析扩展了先前的发现；在数学上，证明了对于投影服从高斯分布的平衡类，OOD AUROC 与参考探测器的 MCS 之间存在线性关系，因为二者均为测试数据信噪比（SNR）的 S 型函数。同时，通过实证验证了该理论在线性关系失效场景下的预测能力。

Result: 证实了 MCS 与 OOD AUROC 之间存在高度线性相关性（R²=0.98），并推导出这种线性关系源于二者共同依赖于信噪比（SNR）的数学结构。此外，明确了在何种条件下该线性关系会失效，从而完善了对探测器性能度量的理论理解。

Conclusion: 马氏余弦相似度（MCS）是衡量线性探测器性能的理论上可靠且经验上有效的指标，能够显著优于传统的欧氏余弦相似度。该研究揭示了探测器泛化性能的线性预测机制，并为解释性研究中的指标选择提供了坚实的理论基础。

Abstract: Linear probes are widely used in interpretability research and often compared by cosine similarity. The Mahalanobis cosine similarity (MCS) between two directions, which reweights the inner product by test data covariance, is a natural task-aware refinement. Ying et al. (2026) report that a probe's MCS to a reference probe trained on the out-of-distribution (OOD) data near-perfectly linearly predicts the probe's OOD AUROC (R^2 = 0.98). Here, we extend this empirical finding across models, layers, and concept domains, and prove this general phenomenon in closed form: For balanced classes whose projections are Gaussian, OOD AUROC and MCS to the reference probe are linear because both are sigmoid-shaped functions of the probe's signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) on the test data. The theory also predicts when this linearity fails, which we verify empirically. MCS offers a theoretically grounded and empirically effective alternative to Euclidean cosine similarity for comparing linear probes.

### [170] [Latent Confounded Causal Discovery via Lie Bracket Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19610)
*Sridhar Mahadevan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于Kan-Do-Calculus范畴论框架的因果发现新范式，利用干预诱导的向量场及其几何性质（李括号残差）来有效推断潜变量结构，极大地缩减了因果模型的搜索空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的因果发现方法在存在潜变量混杂时面临巨大的搜索空间和计算挑战。本研究旨在通过Kan-Do-Calculus（将干预和条件化建模为左/右Kan扩展）提供的范畴论框架，利用干预诱导的几何流信息来直接推断潜在的因果结构，从而突破现有方法的局限。

Method: 提出了两种算法：1. BRIDGE（基于李括号残差的因果发现）：利用观察测度与干预测度间的Radon-Nikodym导数诱导局部因果向量场，通过计算向量场的李括号残差来识别潜在的未建模结构（即不可积性）；2. SKFM（谱Kan-Do流匹配）：学习摊销的干预场，并通过谱分解提取潜在曲率，定位李空间终点。

Result: 实验证明，BRIDGE和SKFM算法在存在潜变量混杂的情况下，能够成功发现因果模型，并将潜在的有向无环图（DAG）搜索空间减少了数个数量级。

Conclusion: 该研究通过结合范畴论中的Kan-Do-Calculus（KDC）与信息几何，提出了一种利用干预诱导流的几何特征来推断潜变量结构的新范式。实验表明，该方法能够有效地在潜变量干扰下发现因果模型，并显著减少搜索空间。

Abstract: Recent work on Kan-Do-Calculus (KDC) has established that the boundary between passive observation and active intervention in causal inference is a category-theoretic bi-adjunction, with interventions modeled by left Kan extensions and conditioning by right Kan extensions. This paper introduces two causal discovery algorithms under latent confounding, building on the information-geometric and categorical consequences of KDC. In smooth statistical settings, Radon-Nikodym derivatives between observational and interventional measures induce local causal vector fields; failures of these fields to close under Lie brackets become computable Frobenius residuals, which we interpret as witnesses of failed visible integrability and possible latent or unmodeled structure. Our first algorithm, BRIDGE (Bracket Residuals for Interventional Discovery and Geometric Estimation), combines an interventional density or Radon-Nikodym-ratio engine with a geometric screen that proposes a high-recall family of admissible arrows, identifies non-closing visible pairs as latent-obstruction candidates, and passes the reduced family to downstream score-based or differentiable discovery routines. The second algorithmic contribution, Spectral Kan-Do Flow Matching (SKFM), learns amortized intervention fields and factors latent curvature spectrally, exposing the direct Lie-space endpoint toward which BRIDGE points. A detailed set of experiments show that both algorithms are capable of discovering causal models with latent confounders while collapsing the super-exponential space of possible DAGs by many orders of magnitude. This paper introduces a new paradigm in causal discovery, where latent structure is inferred directly from the geometry of intervention-induced flows.

### [171] [SEAGAN: domain-Specific and Edge-Aware Graph Attention Network for Dynamic Plant Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19623)

Abstract: Graph neural networks (GNNs) provide a flexible framework for learning from scientific data linked through physical, biological, or functional relationships. One promising domain is plant physiology, where measured responses often arise from multiple interacting processes whose exact separation remains difficult even with manual intervention. Here, we formulate limitation-state identification along A-Ci curves as a graph-based node classification problem, with curve points as nodes. The results show that representing A-Ci curves as graphs improves biochemical limitation-state analysis, with edge-aware attention over local kNN neighborhoods providing the most effective strategy.

Abstract: Reliable benchmarking is critical for developing machine learning models for tandem mass spectrometry (MS/MS) based molecule discovery. We distill our findings into recommendations generalizable to MS/MS challenges, benchmarks, and custom evaluation setups. We also release MassSpecGym v1.5, an implementation of our recommendations in the MassSpecGym benchmarking suite which addresses the failure modes identified in this audit. ### [173] [Hard or Just Unreached? Diagnosing the Sampling Blind Spot in Math-Reasoning Difficulty Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19636)
*Luca Zhou,Sajel Shah,Emanuele Rodolà,Roberto Dessì*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究揭示了以pass@k为核心的推理基准测试在评估高难度数学问题时的盲区，利用激活修补技术成功“找回”了大量原本被误认为模型无法解决的样本，证明了模型内部存在更深层的可解性结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前的数学和科学推理基准测试主要依赖pass@k（通过采样链中达到正确答案的比例）作为衡量题目难度的唯一信号。然而，研究者怀疑这一指标无法全面覆盖模型能力的“最难层级”，即对于那些在有限采样下无法解决的题目，模型是否在内部表征上实际上具备解决能力。

Method: 研究团队提出了一种名为“激活修补”（activation grafting）的诊断工具。该方法在确定性解码（贪婪搜索）的基础上，引入五种廉价的残差流扰动，构建了一个六链的确定性方案。研究通过对比该方案与传统采样（pass@k）在GSM8K和MATH数据集上的表现，分析了被原始采样漏掉的样本在模型内部表征中的结构特性。

Result: 实验显示，在传统的pass@k评估中被标记为0%（即采样六次均无法解答）的样本中，有10.3%到22.9%的题目通过所提出的六链确定性方案被成功求解。相比之下，单纯的贪婪解码只能解决不到6%的题目。这证明了传统的采样方法在识别模型潜能上存在系统性漏判。

Conclusion: 研究表明，现有的pass@k评估指标在衡量高难度数学推理任务时存在显著盲区。通过激活修补技术可以发现并“找回”原本被认为模型无法解决的样本，证明了这些样本在模型的内部表征中具有结构可识别性，而非简单的随机性失败。研究强调了在评估模型能力时，单纯依赖采样率的局限性，并为更深入地理解模型推理失败机制提供了新路径。

Abstract: Math and science reasoning benchmarks rely on pass@k, the fraction of sampled chains that reach gold, as the canonical per-example difficulty signal. The same signal drives RL with verifiable rewards, math data curation, synthetic curricula, and verifier training. We show this proxy has a persistent blind spot on its hardest stratum: on the eight free-form math cells we test (GSM8K and MATH across four open-weight models), 10.3-22.9% of the examples that no sampling seed solves in six tries are instead solved at matched compute by a six-chain deterministic regime. These are greedy decoding plus five cheap residual-stream perturbations applied via activation grafting, while greedy alone solves at most 6% on these math cells. Recovery scales with the additional budget, across perturbations whose mechanistic distinctness we verify across all twelve cells (cross-kind fix-set Jaccard <= 0.47 in every setup). Activation grafting is used as an intervention on internal representations, not a decoding method; we use it purely as a diagnostic and diversification tool, and our recovered items show that the pass@k= 0 % stratum is structurally identifiable in the residual stream rather than that the unmodified model reaches them under ordinary inference.

### [174] [Convex training of Lipschitz-regularized shallow neural networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19652)
*Chao Yin,Antoine Lesage-Landry*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将非凸Lipschitz正则化训练转化为凸优化问题的求解策略，通过保证全局最优性显著提升了浅层神经网络在对抗环境下的鲁棒性和预测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的神经网络容易受到对抗攻击的影响，而针对Lipschitz正则化的非凸优化过程往往难以保证获得全局最优解，导致模型在对抗环境下的稳健性受限。因此，研究者旨在寻找一种能够通过凸优化求解以保证全局最优性的方法，从而提升模型的对抗稳健性。

Method: 提出了一种针对浅层神经网络的训练过程：将原本非凸的Lipschitz正则化问题转化为一个可以高效求解至全局最优的凸限制问题。该方法既可作为一种训练策略，也可作为预训练网络的后处理步骤，通过优化初始模型来进一步提升性能。

Result: 数值实验结果表明，该方法在回归任务中比现有方法能获得更低的Lipschitz正则化目标函数值。同时，在真实数据集上，该方法训练出的网络在对抗攻击下表现出更高的准确率和稳健性。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了通过凸限制（convex restriction）方法求解Lipschitz正则化问题，可以有效提升浅层神经网络在对抗攻击下的鲁棒性。该方法不仅在理论上保证了结果不劣于初始网络，而且在实际应用中展现了在准确率和对抗稳健性方面的双重优势。

Abstract: In this work, we introduce a training procedure for shallow neural networks that promotes robustness against adversarial attacks. We solve a non-convex Lipschitz-regularized training program by introducing a convex restriction that can be efficiently solved to global optimality. Our approach can be employed as a post-processing step by taking a pre-trained network as an initial solution to then solving the convex program whose optimal network is guaranteed to be no worse than the initial one. We illustrate the improvements of our training procedure with experiments using real world datasets for regression tasks under an adversarial setting. We show numerically that solving our proposed convex program yields networks with lower objective values on the Lipschitz-regularized program compared to existing methods. Additionally, we show that on certain datasets, networks obtained using our convex training program are both more accurate and robust with respect to adversarial attacks.

### [175] [LOKI: Memory-Free Null-Space Constrained Lifelong Knowledge Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19679)
*Masih Eskandar,Miquel Sirera Perelló,Stratis Ioannidis,Jennifer Dy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LOKI 是一种创新的长期知识编辑框架，通过动态层选择和零空间梯度投影技术，在无需历史数据的情况下，实现了模型知识的高效更新，并有效缓解了灾难性遗忘。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的长期知识编辑方法存在两大局限：一是固定更新层的做法导致灵活性差且容易引发灾难性遗忘；二是通常依赖于对历史知识数据的访问或广泛的预处理统计信息，在实际应用中难以实现。

Method: 提出了一种名为 LOKI 的新方法，该方法包含两个核心组件：1. 基于希尔伯特-施密特独立性准则（HSIC）的动态层选择机制，根据新知识灵活确定需要更新的模型层；2. 基于零空间投影的梯度更新策略，确保模型权重更新在保持对旧知识影响最小化的前提下进行，从而无需访问历史数据。

Result: 实验结果表明，LOKI 在多种实验设置中均优于现有方法，平均准确率提升高达 14%。

Conclusion: LOKI 通过动态层选择和零空间投影技术，解决了长期知识编辑中的灵活性不足与灾难性遗忘问题，在无需回溯历史数据的情况下，显著提升了模型更新的效率与准确性。

Abstract: Lifelong knowledge editing aims to efficiently and sequentially update language models over time, as new knowledge becomes available or when the model makes mistakes, while preserving acceptable performance on past knowledge. One unresolved challenge is that existing methods modify a fixed set of layers for all new knowledge samples, reducing flexibility and increasing catastrophic forgetting. Another is requiring access to previous knowledge and extensive pre-processing to obtain data statistics. To address these challenges, we introduce LOKI, a novel approach that uses dynamic layer selection based on the Hilbert-Schmidt Independence Criterion and projects gradient updates onto the null-space of the model weights, bypassing the requirement for previous knowledge access. We show that LOKI achieves superior performance to existing approaches across a wide variety of experiments, achieving up to a 14\% improvement in average accuracy.

Subsequently, an adaptive multi-agent reinforcement learning strategy leverages the attention-aware semantic states to optimize personalized web actions like content recommendation, navigation optimization, and service adaptation. ### [177] [Efficiently Representing Algorithms With Chain-of-Thought Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19697)
*Yanhong Li,Anej Svete,Ashish Sabharwal,William Merrill*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文从理论上证明了思维链Transformer能够以极高的效率（多对数开销）模拟Word RAM模型中的算法，证明了其执行通用、高效算法的强大能力，超越了传统图灵机模拟的效率瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然现有研究已证明思维链Transformer可以模拟图灵机，但图灵机模型在算法设计与分析中缺乏直观性和效率。Word RAM模型是算法领域的主流抽象模型，本文旨在探讨CoT Transformer是否能够高效地模拟Word RAM算法，从而更准确地评估推理模型在复杂算法执行上的能力边界。

Method: 研究团队通过构造性证明，展示了在三种特定Transformer架构（具有多对数宽度和右侧唯一硬注意力机制的有限精度Transformer、连续CoT架构、以及基于线性RNN的混合架构）下，如何将Word RAM的计算步骤映射为Transformer的推理过程，并量化了该模拟过程的开销。

Result: 研究结果表明，CoT Transformer能够以多项式对数级的开销高效模拟任何Word RAM算法。在特定条件下（如“扁平”指令集），该开销可进一步降低至对数平方或线性对数级别。这显著优于以往将Transformer视为图灵机模拟器的二次方开销结论。

Conclusion: 本文证明了思维链（CoT）Transformer不仅理论上能模拟图灵机，还能高效地模拟Word RAM模型。这一结论弥合了深度学习推理模型与经典算法复杂度理论之间的鸿沟，证明了Transformer具备执行高效算法的能力，且在多项式对数开销下具有通用性。

Abstract: The increasing popularity of \emph{reasoning} models -- language models that output a series of reasoning or thought tokens before producing an answer -- is justified, in part, by theoretical results showing that chain-of-thought (CoT) transformers can simulate Turing machines, and thus perform arbitrary computation. However, the Turing machine, while suitable for complexity-theoretic analysis, is not convenient, intuitive, or efficient for discussing algorithms. Algorithms are typically designed and analyzed at a higher level of abstraction, captured by the \emph{Word RAM} model with random-access memory and unit-cost operations on $\bigO(\log n)$-bit words. As a result, Word RAM algorithms can be substantially more efficient than their Turing machine counterparts, raising the question: \emph{Can CoT transformers efficiently simulate Word RAM algorithms?} For instance, can they sort $n$ items in $\bigO(n \log n)$ steps or run Dijkstra's algorithm in $\bigO(E + V \log V)$ steps? We answer affirmatively, up to poly-logarithmic overhead. We first establish this for finite-precision transformers with poly-logarithmic width and rightmost unique hard attention, then strengthen the result to two more practical settings with finite width and log-precision: \emph{continuous} CoT, where reasoning takes the form of vectors rather than tokens, and a \emph{hybrid} architecture in which transformer layers sit atop a recurrent (linear RNN) layer. In all three cases, we find that CoT \emph{can} efficiently simulate any Word RAM algorithm with only a poly-logarithmic overhead in $n$. This overhead reduces to log-square when the Word RAM has a ``flat'' instruction set, and only logarithmic for multiplication-free flat instructions -- in stark contrast to known CoT simulations of Turing machines, which require quadratic overhead over Word RAM.

### [178] [Efficient Neural Network Model Selection for Few-Class Application Datasets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19712)
*Bryan Bo Cao,Abhinav Sharma,Lawrence O'Gorman,Michael Coss,Shubham Jain*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对少类别任务，提出了一种名为“少类区分度”的数据属性度量方法，显著提升了资源受限场景下模型选择和优化的效率，实现了模型性能与计算成本的优化平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前的高性能神经网络研究多集中在海量类别数据集，但许多实际边缘计算应用（如机器人、无人机）仅涉及极少数类别。现有基准测试方法在这些场景下效率低下，缺乏利用数据特性来指导高效模型选择的机制。

Method: 提出了一种基于数据侧属性的分类难度度量方法，称为“少类区分度”（few-class distinctiveness）。通过该指标，可以在无需完整训练和测试模型的情况下，直接评估模型在少类别数据集上的适应性，并据此对模型架构进行裁剪和优化。

Result: 该方法在模型选择上的速度比传统反复训练测试快 6 到 29 倍；通过扩展模型缩放策略，在少类别任务中实现了比现有小模型（如 YOLOv5-nano）体积缩小达 42% 的高性能模型，且在多个边缘计算应用场景中保持了精度。

Conclusion: 研究表明，利用“少类区分度”这一数据属性，可以有效预测模型在少类别任务中的性能，从而为资源受限的边缘计算场景提供了一种无需反复训练即可进行高效模型选择的实用方案。

Abstract: While much effort has focused on developing and benchmarking high-performance neural networks, less attention has been given to how dataset properties, known to practitioners, can guide efficient model selection. Neural models are typically evaluated on datasets with thousands of classes, yet many real-world applications involve fewer than ten. To address this understudied but common setting, we develop a measure of classification difficulty based on data-side properties and show how it enables more efficient model selection for few-class datasets, where traditional approaches are less effective. We term this phenomenon "few-class distinctiveness". Our metric allows comparison of models and datasets 6 to 29$\times$ faster than repeated training and testing. Leveraging this insight, we extend scaled model families below the smallest published models, achieving greater efficiency at similar accuracy, for example models up to 42% smaller than YOLOv5-nano for a mobile robot task. Targeting resource-constrained applications, we demonstrate few-class model selection across mobile robot, drone, and IoT scenarios, highlighting practical gains in efficiency without sacrificing performance.

</details>

Method: 本研究提出了 OnDeFog 框架，该方法将原有的 DeFog（针对随机帧丢失优化的离线决策 Transformer）中的机制与在线决策 Transformer（ODT）相结合，通过直接与环境交互进行策略学习，使其不仅能处理帧丢失问题，还能适应训练数据中未覆盖的新状态。

Result: 实验结果表明，OnDeFog 在高帧丢失率的环境中明显优于 ODT，且在包含大量低质量（低奖励）数据的数据集中，其表现优于离线方法 DeFog，证明了其在处理帧丢失和泛化能力上的显著优势。

Conclusion: OnDeFog 有效结合了脱机学习中应对帧丢失的机制与在线学习的实时交互能力，填补了现有方法在处理帧丢失及面对新状态时的性能缺口，为复杂现实环境下的强化学习提供了一种鲁棒性更强、泛化能力更好的解决方案。

Abstract: In challenging real-world reinforcement learning applications, communication delays or sensor failures often cause frame dropping, in which the agent cannot receive the dropped states and associated rewards. To address the performance degradation caused by frame dropping, the Decision Transformer under Random Frame Dropping (DeFog) was developed by incorporating additional mechanisms into the decision transformer to tackle frame dropping. Although DeFog can mitigate performance degradation in frame-dropping environments, since DeFog is an offline learning method, it struggles to effectively generalize to novel states not adequately represented in the training dataset. In this study, we propose OnDeFog, which integrates the mechanisms in DeFog with the online decision transformer (ODT), an online reinforcement learning method that learns policies through direct environmental interaction. Comprehensive experimental evaluation demonstrates that our proposed OnDeFog achieves superior performance compared to ODT in environments characterized by high dropping frame rate and outperforms DeFog on datasets containing a large amount of low-reward data.

We study federated bilevel performative prediction, where both upper-level (UL) and lower-level (LL) objectives are evaluated under client-dependent, decision-dependent distributions. *Darrien McKenzie,Nicklas Hansen,Xiaolong Wang*

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为“贝叶斯流形课程”（BMC）的框架，通过将问题采样建模为具有结构特性的多臂老虎机问题，利用任务间的层次结构和模型潜在空间关系，优化强化学习中的训练问题采样，从而更有效地提升大语言模型的推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了“贝叶斯流形课程”（Bayesian Manifold Curriculum, BMC）框架：1. 将问题组织成层次化的任务树结构；2. 将问题采样建模为带有内源性非平稳性的“流形结构化多臂老虎机”问题；3. 利用贝叶斯学习来指导采样决策，以平衡学习信号的生产力、任务空间覆盖的多样性以及评估相关性。

Result: 实验结果表明，不同的采样策略会在生产力（学习信号）、多样性（任务流形覆盖）和效用（评估相关性）之间产生权衡。相比于传统的难度优先采样，BMC框架能更有效地捕捉任务空间结构，显著提升模型在下游任务中的表现。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，仅依靠难度进行采样对于提升大语言模型的推理能力是不够的，必须将任务的结构化属性和类型感知纳入考虑。BMC框架证明了在强化学习中利用任务流形结构能更有效地引导模型学习，从而在生产力、多样性和效用之间实现更好的平衡。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) is a central approach for improving reasoning capabilities in large language models (LLMs), where training efficiency depends critically on how problems are sampled during optimization. Existing adaptive curriculum learning methods typically prioritize prompts of intermediate difficulty, treating problem selection as a standard bandit problem with independent arms and overlooking the structured, heterogeneous nature of the task space. In this work, we frame problem sampling as a manifold-structured bandit problem with endogenous non-stationarity: problems are related through the model's latent representation space, and sampling decisions can steer how learning signals evolve across that space. To operationalize this perspective, we introduce Bayesian Manifold Curriculum (BMC), a structure-aware framework that organizes problems into a hierarchical task tree and applies Bayesian learning to guide sampling. Empirically, we find that different sampling strategies induce non-trivial tradeoffs between productivity (learning signal), diversity (coverage of the task manifold), and utility (evaluation relevance). These results show that prioritizing difficulty alone is insufficient for strong downstream performance, highlighting the importance of incorporating structure and type-awareness into problem sampling.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Partial differential equations (PDEs) play a central role in modeling complex physical, biological, and engineering systems. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种基于信息论的图数据新颖性生成框架：首先将数据嵌入到潜空间，利用有限混合模型对潜分布进行建模；其次，通过引入描述长度（Description Length）量化新颖性和可靠性条件，强制生成模型产生现有混合分量难以解释且符合最小描述长度（MDL）原则的样本。

Conclusion: 本文提出的信息论框架为图数据的创新生成提供了一种可量化风险的原则性方法，能够在保证全局结构一致性的前提下有效地生成具有新颖性的样本，并通过理论证明了该方法在错误分类风险上的收敛性。

Abstract: We propose an information-theoretic framework for graph novelty generation, which aims to generate data that are distinct from existing patterns while preserving global structural consistency. Our approach embeds data into a latent space, models the latent distribution using finite mixture models, and generates novel samples by imposing explicit novelty and reliability conditions formulated in terms of description length. Specifically, novelty is enforced by requiring generated samples to be poorly explained by all existing mixture components, while reliability constrains their impact on the overall mixture structure under the Minimum Description Length (MDL) principle. We provide a theoretical analysis showing that, with appropriate threshold choices, the probabilities of misclassifying non-novel or unreliable samples converge to zero with explicit rates. Experiments on synthetic and benchmark graph datasets demonstrate that the proposed method enables principled novelty generation with quantifiable risk.

### [184] [Flow Map Denoisers: Traversing the Distortion-Perception Plane for Inverse Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19802)
*Nicolas Zilberstein,Morteza Mardani,Santiago Segarra*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出利用流图模型中的“前瞻参数”作为调节旋钮，无需重新训练即可在图像恢复任务中自由平衡失真与感知质量，解决了图像恢复领域长期的权衡难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 图像恢复领域长期存在“失真-感知”权衡问题：最小化误差的方法往往导致图像模糊，而最大化感知质量的方法虽锐利但保真度不足。现有方法通常需要在二者间做出取舍，或依赖复杂的辅助模型与超参数调整，缺乏一种简单且灵活的统一框架。

Method: 研究者利用流匹配（Flow Matching）的扩展——流图模型，发现其学习到的平均场隐含地定义了一个单参数去噪器家族。通过引入前瞻参数（Lookahead parameter）t，将其作为控制失真与感知平衡的“调节旋钮”，并将其集成到即插即用（Plug-and-Play）求解器中，以应对通用的图像逆问题。

Result: 对于高斯目标，理论上证明了该方法能准确复现最优失真-感知边界；在自然图像实验中，单一流图模型不仅在失真和感知两个极端表现优于或持平于专用基线方法，还成功处理了多种线性与非线性逆问题。

Conclusion: 本文证明了流图模型（Flow Map Models）提供了一种无需额外训练或复杂超参数调整的有效方式，能够通过单一模型在失真-感知（Distortion-Perception）边界上进行平滑切换，为图像恢复任务提供了一种统一且灵活的解决方案。

Abstract: Image restoration faces a fundamental tradeoff: methods that minimize error produce blurry reconstructions, while those that maximize perceptual quality yield sharp but less faithful images. Existing approaches either commit to a single operating point on this distortion perception (DP) frontier or require paired-data supervision, auxiliary models, or hyperparameter tuning of the sampler to access different points. We show that flow map models, a recent extension of flow matching for few-step sampling that learns an average field, implicitly define a one-parameter family of denoisers that continuously spans the DP frontier. The lookahead parameter t acts as a control knob between the MMSE and perceptual regimes. For Gaussian targets, we prove that varying t exactly recovers the optimal DP frontier; for natural images, we observe similar behavior empirically. Within a Plug-and-Play solver, the same mechanism extends to general inverse problems, where it controls a tradeoff between perceptual alignment and data consistency. Despite the lack of exact optimality guarantees in this setting, a single trained flow map spans the DP tradeoff, matching or exceeding specialized baselines at both extremes. Extensive experiments on CelebA ($128\times 128$) and AFHQ ($256\times 256$) across several linear and nonlinear inverse tasks validate our findings.

### [185] [Uncertainty-Aware Reward Modeling for Stable RLHF](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19818)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 RLHF 流程存在两大缺陷：一是奖励模型作为确定性估计器，缺乏对预测置信度的感知；二是 GRPO 等策略优化算法会放大不可靠的奖励信号，导致模型在探索过程中出现严重的“奖励欺骗”（Reward Hacking）。

Method: 提出不确定性感知奖励建模（UARM），利用基于分位数的共形预测（Conformal Prediction）对奖励模型进行不确定性校准，并结合异方差方差分解方法，对 GRPO 的优势函数进行加权处理，以降低不可靠奖励信号的影响。

Result: 在 HelpSteer、UltraFeedback 和 PKU-SafeRLHF 数据集上的实验结果表明，UARM 显著提升了奖励模型的校准能力，减少了奖励欺骗现象，并在下游对齐质量上超越了标准 GRPO 及其他不考虑不确定性的基线方法。

Conclusion: UARM 框架通过引入不确定性量化与优势函数加权，有效缓解了 RLHF 中的奖励欺骗问题，为训练更安全、更鲁棒的对齐模型提供了有效手段。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) aligns large language models by training reward models on preference data and optimizing policies to maximize predicted rewards. However, this pipeline faces two fundamental challenges: (1) reward models cannot signal when their predictions are unreliable, since they usually act as deterministic point estimators; and (2) modern group-based policy optimization can amplify unreliable reward signals, as exemplified by GRPO's uniform treatment of rewards during advantage computation. As policies explore increasingly diverse responses, these two limitations create a critical vulnerability: unreliable reward estimates may be granted disproportionate influence, triggering severe reward hacking. We propose Uncertainty-Aware Reward Modeling (UARM), which equips reward models with calibrated uncertainty via quantile-based conformal prediction and reweights GRPO advantages through heteroscedastic variance decomposition. Experiments across HelpSteer, UltraFeedback, and PKU-SafeRLHF demonstrate that UARM significantly improves reward model calibration, reduces reward hacking, and enhances downstream alignment quality compared to standard GRPO and uncertainty-agnostic baselines.

Abstract: Accurate prediction of dust source emissions is critical for mitigating the significant environmental and health hazards posed by dust storms. Traditional forecasting methods often struggle to capture the complex spatiotemporal dynamics of these phenomena.
  In this paper, we demonstrate that proximity graphs enable Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) to effectively model the intricate spatial and temporal relationships between data points. Specifically, we use proximity graphs--such as Delaunay triangulation, Gabriel graph, k-Nearest Neighbor graph, and Yao graph--as the input for GNNs (including GraphSAGE, Graph Convolutional Networks, and Graph Attention Networks) to perform message passing.
  Our approach highlights the effectiveness of integrating proximity graphs with GNNs for robust and accurate dust source forecasting. To emphasize the importance of proximity graph representations, we compare our method against GNNs using random graphs for message passing. The results show that GNNs with proximity graphs significantly outperform those with random graphs and are also far superior to Long Short-Term Memory (LSTM) model in dust source emission forecasting.

### [187] [When, Where, and How: Adaptive Binning for Tabular Self-Supervised Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19827)

Method: 提出一种“自适应分箱”（Adaptive Binning）预训练方法。该方法采用特征维度的由粗到细（coarse-to-fine）课程学习策略，根据模型训练状态动态调整分箱方案；结合表征感知的分裂策略，统一了分类重构与数值特征的序数监督；利用异构感知目标函数处理医学数据中常见的混合数据类型。

Abstract: Medical tabular data are ubiquitous in clinical research, but deep learning for tables remains underexplored because reliable labels often require costly expert adjudication, even though structured clinical variables are routinely available in tabular form. Self-supervised learning can leverage these unlabeled tables, and recent binning-based pretexts offer a promising inductive bias, but existing objectives fix a single global quantile discretization and apply feature-agnostic supervision. We propose Adaptive Binning, a training-adaptive discretization pretext for tabular SSL that couples discretization to learning through a feature-wise coarse-to-fine curriculum. Motivated by the spectral bias of neural networks and the principles of curriculum learning, our method progressively refines discretization per feature upon plateau detection and selects representation-aware splits to jointly improve value-space concentration and representation-space coherence. A heterogeneity-aware objective unifies categorical reconstruction with ordinal supervision for numerical features, and experiments on public medical tabular datasets under unified evaluation protocols show consistent gains for linear probing and fine-tuning without dataset-specific discretization tuning. We further introduce a medical tabular SSL benchmark with standardized protocols to support reproducible progress in this underexplored domain. Our code is available at https://github.com/labhai/Adaptive-Binning.

This paper proposes incorporating the feature selection mechanism into NAM and NBM to resolve computational bottlenecks. We introduce the feature selection layer in both models and update the selection weights during training. Our method is simple and can reduce computational costs and model sizes compared to vanilla NAM and NBM. In addition, it enables us to use two-input NNs even in high-dimensional datasets and capture feature interactions. ### [190] [Global Convergence of Gradient Descent for Score Matching in Gaussian Mixtures via Reverse Fisher Divergence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19876)
*Alexander Tyurin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出利用逆向Fisher散度优化高斯混合模型（GMM）以克服传统正向Fisher散度的收敛缺陷，并从理论上证明了该目标函数在特定条件下可保证全局收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代生成模型（如扩散模型）常用的正向Fisher散度在简单高斯混合模型场景下，存在收敛行为不理想且高度依赖初始化的缺陷。为了解决这一问题，作者提出研究逆向Fisher散度（即期望值相对于学生分布进行计算），以寻找更优的优化目标函数。

Method: 本文采用基于Lyapunov函数的梯度下降（GD）动力学分析方法。研究分别在单高斯目标分布和GMM目标分布下，分析了学生模型参数通过GD更新的行为。对于GMM目标分布，在假设教师均值具有$\widetilde{\Omega}(1)$分离度的情况下，证明了全局随机初始化下的收敛性。

Result: 研究结果表明：1. 当教师为单高斯、学生为固定权值和单位协方差的GMM时，GD可从任意初始化实现全局收敛；2. 当教师亦为GMM时，在满足特定分离度假设下，GD能以高概率实现学生组件向最近教师组件的收敛，且学生分布在全变分距离下收敛。

Conclusion: 本文证明了逆向Fisher散度相比于传统的正向Fisher散度具有更优的优化地形，为高斯混合模型（GMM）学习提供了全局收敛的理论保证，克服了正向Fisher散度在训练中的初始化依赖和收敛不佳问题。

Abstract: The score matching problem is a central training objective in modern generative modeling, diffusion models, fitting unnormalized statistical models, and inverse problems. A standard approach is to minimize the forward Fisher divergence, where the expectation is taken with respect to the teacher distribution. However, recent results show that even in simple Gaussian mixture model settings, this objective can lead to undesirable and initialization-dependent convergence behavior. In this paper, we study an alternative objective: the reverse Fisher divergence, where the expectation is taken with respect to the student distribution. We analyze gradient descent (GD) for fitting Gaussian mixture models and show that this change in the objective leads to significantly better optimization properties. First, when the teacher distribution is a single Gaussian and the student is a Gaussian mixture model with fixed weights and identity covariances, we prove the global convergence of GD from arbitrary initializations. Second, we extend the analysis to the case where the teacher is also a Gaussian mixture model and prove global convergence guarantees under a global random initialization scheme and a $\widetildeΩ(1)$-separation assumption on the target means. In particular, with high probability, each student component converges near its closest teacher component, and we provide conditions under which the student distribution converges in total variation distance. Our proofs rely on a new Lyapunov-based analysis of the gradient descent dynamics, showing that the reverse Fisher divergence has a much more favorable optimization landscape than the forward Fisher divergence.

### [191] [On the Oracle Complexity of Interpolation-Based Gradient Descent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19878)
*Dongmin Lee,William Lu,Anuran Makur*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用训练数据平滑性来近似梯度的优化算法 PPI-GD，通过分段多项式插值显著提升了特定条件下的算法预言机复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的经验风险最小化（ERM）优化研究指出，利用训练数据空间上的损失函数平滑性（而非参数空间的平滑性）可以提升梯度下降方法的预言机复杂度，旨在探索利用该特性改进优化效率的算法。

Method: 提出了一种名为“分段多项式插值梯度下降”（PPI-GD）的非精确梯度法。该方法通过在数据域的等距点查询一阶预言机，构造分段多项式插值来近似每一轮迭代中的全梯度。研究针对强凸和非凸损失函数进行了预言机复杂度分析，并引入了多变量张量积多项式插值误差分析技术。

Result: 理论分析表明，在数据空间维度受训练样本数量的多对数函数限制且损失函数足够平滑的情况下，PPI-GD 的预言机复杂度优于多种现有的梯度下降变体。此外，研究提供的多变量张量积多项式插值误差分析具有一定的独立学术价值。

Conclusion: PPI-GD 方法通过在数据域上利用分段多项式插值近似梯度，有效地降低了在平滑损失函数下的预言机复杂度，特别是在低维数据场景下展现出优于传统梯度下降变体的性能。该研究同时拓展了多变量张量积多项式插值的误差分析理论。

Abstract: Recent work on first-order optimizers for empirical risk minimization (ERM) has suggested that smoothness of ERM loss functions in the training data, rather than in the optimization parameters, can be leveraged to improve the oracle complexity of gradient descent (GD) methods. In this paper, we propose an inexact gradient method, piecewise polynomial interpolation-based gradient descent (PPI-GD), which approximates the full gradient in each iteration by querying the first-order oracle at equidistant points in the data domain to construct polynomial interpolants of the resulting gradient samples over appropriately sized patches of the data domain. We analyze the oracle complexity of PPI-GD for strongly convex and non-convex loss functions when the data space dimension is bounded by a polylogarithmic function of the number of training samples, and find it to outperform several GD variants in key regimes when the loss function is sufficiently smooth. Furthermore, our analysis extends several techniques from the error analysis of bicubic spline interpolants to the setting of $d$-variate tensor product polynomial interpolants which may be of independent interest in interpolation analysis.

### [192] [Matching Markets meet Cumulative Prospect Theory: Towards Optimal and Adversarially Robust Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19883)
*Ananya Kunisetty,Avishek Ghosh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了基于累积前景理论（CPT）的人类偏好驱动下的多智能体匹配博弈，提出了能够消除K依赖的最优算法，并实现了在对抗性环境下的鲁棒后悔控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统多智能体匹配市场模型通常假设智能体是完全理性的，而现实中人类决策往往存在行为偏好偏差。为了更准确地模拟人类在风险决策下的偏好（特别是利用在行为经济学中广泛应用的累积前景理论），研究者试图解决受行为偏差影响下的多智能体多臂老虎机博弈问题。

Method: 1. 使用累积前景理论（CPT）中具有α-Hölder连续性的权重函数来模拟人类偏好；2. 采用针对性的探索策略，通过审慎选择活跃臂集合（active set of arms）来优化后悔界，从而消除对臂数量K的强依赖；3. 在对抗性市场模型中，分别针对已知和未知奖励污染预算的情况，提出了鲁棒学习算法。

Result: 1. 在CPT权重扭曲奖励下，推导出智能体最优后悔界为 O(Klog T (1/Δ)^(2/α))；2. 通过优化探索策略，消除了主要项中对臂数量K的依赖，在K远大于智能体数量N的场景下实现了最优后悔界；3. 在对抗性市场中，针对已知和未知污染预算，均实现了对数级的智能体最优后悔界。

Conclusion: 该研究成功将累积前景理论（CPT）引入多智能体多臂老虎机问题，并在考虑人类偏好偏斜的情况下，推导出了最优后悔界。该工作为处理具有行为偏差的复杂匹配市场提供了理论基础，并在存在对抗性扰动的情况下证明了算法的鲁棒性。

Abstract: We study a multi-agent multi-armed bandit problem in the competitive setup with two-sided matching markets under a human centric decision making model. To capture human preferences, we use cumulative prospect theory (CPT) that weighs the actions of the agent in a nonlinear fashion using a ($α$-Hölder continuous) weight function. CPT has been widely used in behavioral economics and risk sensitive machine learning to emulate human preferences. We analyze the state-of-the-art learning algorithm with CPT weight distorted rewards and obtain a player optimal regret of $\mathcal{O}(K\log T \left(\frac{1}Δ\right)^{2/α})$, where $K$ denotes the number of arms, $T$ is the learning horizon, and $Δ$ represents (suitably defined) players' minimum preference gap. Noticing the dependence on $Δ$ to be sub-optimal, we further improve this regret by judiciously selecting the active set of arms during exploration, which removes the dependence on $K$ in the dominant term and achieves an improved (optimal) regret guarantees in the setting where the number of arms $K$ is significantly larger than the number of players $N$. In addition, we consider adversarial markets where the observed rewards of the agents may be corrupted. We propose and analyze algorithms for robust markets with CPT as risk sensitive measure in both settings where the total corruption budget is known and where it is unknown, and establish logarithmic player-optimal regret guarantees in both cases.

### [193] [SL-S4Wave: Self-Supervised Learning of Physiological Waveforms with Structured State Space Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19888)
*Feng Wu,Harsh Deep,Eric Lehman,Sanyam Kapoor,Guoshuai Zhao,Rahul Krishnan,Gari Clifford,Li-wei H Lehman*

Abstract: Modeling long-sequence medical time series data, such as electrocardiograms (ECG), poses significant challenges due to high sampling rates, multichannel signal complexity, inherent noise, and limited labeled data. While recent self-supervised learning (SSL) methods, based on various encoder architectures such as convolutional neural networks, have been proposed to learn representations from unlabeled data, they often fall short in capturing long-range dependencies and noise-invariant features. Structured state space models (S4) excel at long-sequence modeling, but existing S4 architectures fail to capture the unique characteristics of multichannel physiological waveforms. In this work, we propose SL-S4Wave, a self-supervised learning framework that combines contrastive learning with a tailored encoder built on structured state space models. The encoder incorporates multi-layer global convolution using multiscale subkernels, enabling the capture of both fine-grained local patterns and long-range temporal dependencies in noisy, high-resolution multichannel waveforms. Extensive experiments on real-world datasets demonstrate that SL-S4Wave (1) consistently outperforms state-of-the-art supervised and self-supervised baselines in a challenging arrhythmia detection task, (2) achieves high performance with significantly fewer labeled examples, showcasing strong label efficiency, and (3) maintains robust performance on long waveform segments, highlighting its capacity to model complex temporal dynamics in long sequences that most existing approaches fail to efficiently model, and (4) transfers effectively to unseen arrhythmia types, underscoring its robust cross-domain generalization.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的对抗性多臂老虎机研究大多局限于线性损失函数，而现实世界的损失函数往往是非凸且非光滑的。为了弥补这一理论空白，本研究旨在探索在存在全局预算约束的对抗性扰动下，针对更广泛的凸且β-光滑损失函数如何实现有效的决策与后悔控制。

Method: 研究者改进了标准的土匪优化（Bandit Optimization）算法，引入了针对对抗性扰动的控制策略，通过对扰动累积预算的显式建模，推导并证明了相应的期望后悔界（Expected Regret Bounds）。该分析方法能够有效量化干扰对算法性能的影响，并在干扰归零时自然退化为标准凸优化问题的结论。

Result: 成功建立了一套通用的期望后悔分析框架，明确刻画了扰动预算对最终 regret 的具体影响。在无干扰的理想情况下，该算法的 regret 性能与现有的针对β-光滑损失函数的标准土匪优化算法一致。

Conclusion: 本研究通过将全局预算干扰模型推广至更广泛的凸且β-光滑损失函数类别，证明了在对抗性扰动环境下，学习者依然能够获得可控的期望后悔界，为非凸非光滑的对抗性多臂老虎机问题提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: We study adversarial bandit optimization in which the loss functions may be non-convex and non-smooth. In each round, the learner selects an action and observes only the loss incurred at that action. The loss consists of an underlying convex and $β$-smooth component and an adversarial perturbation that may be chosen after observing the learner's action. The perturbations are subject to a global budget controlling their cumulative magnitude over time.
  This framework extends the globally budgeted, post-action perturbation model from underlying linear losses to general convex and $β$-smooth losses. For this broader class, we establish expected regret guarantees that explicitly characterize the effect of the perturbation budget.
  To establish these guarantees, we modify a standard bandit optimization algorithm and develop an analysis that controls the additional regret caused by the perturbations. In the absence of perturbations, our results reduce to regret guarantees for the standard bandit convex optimization setting with $β$-smooth losses.

</details>


### [195] [Score Approximation for Diffusion Models on Arbitrary Low-Dimensional Structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19894)
*Xinhe Mu,Zaijiu Shang,Zhaoqi Zhou,Chuan Zhou,Qi Meng,Guiying Yan,Zhiming Ma*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文打破了扩散模型评分逼近理论对数据分布光滑性的依赖，证明了即使在具有复杂非光滑结构的数据上，ReLU网络也能高效地逼近评分函数，从而解释了扩散模型处理真实数据的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的评分逼近理论过于依赖Lipschitz连续密度或光滑流形支持等限制性假设，无法涵盖真实世界数据中常见的复杂非光滑结构，导致理论与扩散模型在实际应用中的巨大成功之间存在缺口。

Method: 提出了一种基于ReLU网络的通用评分逼近定理，并采用了新颖的离散混合（discrete-mixture）公式，将评分函数的逼近复杂度与数据分布的上闵可夫斯基维数（upper Minkowski dimension）相关联，而非依赖于环境空间的维度。

Result: 证明了使用ReLU网络可以在上闵可夫斯基维数为d的任意紧集上逼近评分函数，其复杂度仅随d呈指数增长，从而克服了环境维度带来的维数灾难。

Conclusion: 本文证明了扩散模型能够处理具有奇异性、尖锐边界和不连续簇等特征的真实世界复杂数据，为扩散模型在实际生成任务中的卓越表现提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: The remarkable success of score-based diffusion models has spurred significant efforts to establish their theoretical foundations. However, existing complexity bounds for score approximation rely heavily on restrictive assumptions like Lipschitz continuous densities or smooth manifold supports, which are routinely violated by the singularities, sharp boundaries, and disjoint clusters inherent to real-world perceptual data. This work establishes a universal score approximation theorem that works for any distribution supported on any compact set of upper Minkowski dimension $d$. Using a novel discrete-mixture formulation, we prove that the score function can be approximated with a ReLU network whose complexity grows exponentially only with $d$, thus breaking the exponential curse of ambient dimensionality. Combined with existing theories on accurately solving the backward diffusion SDE for arbitrary compact distributions, our work shows that diffusion models readily adapt to irregular, non-smooth data structures, explaining their competence in real-world generative tasks.

### [196] [ADaPT: Token-Level Decoupling for Efficient Large Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19919)
*Tingyun Li,Zishang Jiang,Jinyi Han,Xinyi Wang,Sihang Jiang,Han Xia,Zhaoqian Dai,Shuguang Ma,Fei Yu,Jiaqing Liang,Yanghua Xiao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大型模型长思维链计算开销大的问题，本文提出了ADaPT框架，通过引入模式选择标记将效率与正确性优化解耦，实现了推理成本的显著降低与性能权衡的动态可控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型推理模型依赖长思维链（CoT）以获取强大性能，但统一使用长推理会导致计算开销过大。现有方法虽试图通过缩短或混合策略来提升效率，但往往会导致推理能力下降，其根本原因在于训练过程中效率激励与正确性优化在序列层面的耦合，导致对长推理路径产生了隐式负面惩罚。

Method: 提出了一种自适应双过程思维框架（ADaPT）。该方法引入了“模式选择标记（mode-selection token）”，用于动态控制快速和慢速推理路径；在训练过程中，仅将效率奖励应用于该标记，从而避免对正确但较长的推理路径进行惩罚；在推理时，通过调整该标记的生成概率，实现对推理效率与性能权衡的实时、精确控制。

Result: 广泛的实验表明，ADaPT在保持强大推理性能的同时，显著降低了多种基准测试中的推理计算成本，并且能够让单一模型在推理时平滑地在效率-性能帕累托前沿上移动。

Conclusion: ADaPT通过显式解耦效率与正确性优化，证明了在不牺牲推理能力的前提下，通过自适应模式选择降低大型推理模型计算成本的可行性，为实现更高效、可控的推理模型提供了一种通用且有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Large reasoning models rely on long chain-of-thought to achieve strong performance, but applying such reasoning uniformly incurs high computational cost. Existing efficiency-oriented methods attempt to shorten or mix reasoning strategies, yet often degrade reasoning capability. We identify the root cause as sequence-level coupling between efficiency incentives and correctness optimization, which implicitly penalizes long but correct reasoning trajectories. To address this issue, we propose Adaptive Dual-Process Thinking (ADaPT), a token-level dual-process framework that explicitly decouples efficiency and correctness signals during training. ADaPT introduces a mode-selection token to control fast and slow reasoning, applying efficiency-related rewards exclusively to this token to avoid penalizing correct long reasoning while encouraging efficiency when appropriate. Moreover, ADaPT enables precise and continuous control over the efficiency-performance trade-off at inference time: by adjusting the generation probability of the mode-selection token, a single trained model can smoothly move along the efficiency-performance Pareto frontier. Extensive experiments demonstrate that ADaPT significantly reduces inference cost while maintaining strong reasoning performance across multiple benchmarks.

</details>


### [197] [Compositionality Emerges in a Narrow Depth-Connectivity Regime: Architecture Constraints and Solution Manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19941)
*Dat H. Do,Rushi Shah,Duc V. Le,Dianbo Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文发现神经网络的组合泛化能力依赖于特定的深度与连接性区间。若模型结构不当，训练会趋向于碎片化解。作者通过相似度剪枝和深度预测策略，成功引导模型涌现出组合性，并从理论上解释了这一现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 组合性被视为模型泛化的基石，然而标准梯度优化训练出的模型往往缺乏稳健的组合内部结构。研究者旨在探究组合性在神经网络中形成的具体机制，以及为何深度与连接性会影响其涌现。

Method: 1. 实证分析：通过改变网络的稀疏结构（连接性）与层数（深度），探究组合性出现的临界条件。2. 算法创新：提出相似度剪枝（Similarity-based Pruning, SP）以恢复 compositional 结构；开发启发式深度预测器来估算组合性涌现的最佳深度。3. 理论建模：建立基于组合稀疏性、体积比论证及特征干扰界限的理论框架，解释为何只有在特定窄带区间内才能达到组合解。

Result: 研究发现组合性呈现明显的“深度-连接性”甜点效应：连接性上，关键在于保留哪些连接而非单纯的稀疏度；深度上，存在特定目标依赖的最佳深度区间。若偏离这些条件，模型往往会陷入“碎片化”解而非组合解。实验证明，利用所提出的方法能有效引导模型获得更强的组合特性。

Conclusion: 论文通过实证与理论分析揭示了组合性并非模型训练的必然结果，而是存在于特定的“深度-连接性”窄带区间。研究表明，通过模拟稀疏性与深度预测可以显著提升模型表现，为设计具备强组合泛化能力的神经网络提供了新的指导原则。

Abstract: Compositionality is believed to be the foundation for generalization, enabling models to reuse meaningful primitives in novel combinations. Yet, models trained with standard gradient-based optimization rarely, and often only weakly, exhibit compositional internal structure, and it remains unclear how or why such compositionality forms. In this work, we show that compositionality emerges in a narrow connectivity-depth sweet spot. Along the connectivity axis, compositionality only appears in some specifically sparse networks, heavily depends on which connections remain rather than on weights' sparsity alone. Along the depth axis, compositionality emerges within a narrow, target-dependent regime, peaking at specific depths, while both shallower and deeper networks fail. When either the depth or connectivity condition is violated, gradient descent silently converges to fractured solutions rather than compositional ones. To discover and exploit this emergence, we introduce (i) similarity-based pruning (SP) to recover compositional connectivity and (ii) a heuristic depth predictor to estimate where compositionality is most likely to appear. Finally, we support these empirical findings with a theoretical framework based on compositional sparsity, volume-ratio arguments, and feature-interference bounds, explaining why compositional solutions are reachable only in a narrow depth-connectivity regime.

Beyond quantitative performance, the results highlight that aggregation poses greater complexity and challenges than simplification, underscoring the difficulty of capturing higher-level spatial relationships in map generalization with current deep learning approaches. Although limitations such as data imbalance and the need for post-processing remain, the study provides valuable insights and methodological directions for advancing automated map generalization with deep learning approaches.

Abstract: Tsetlin Machine (TM) is a logic-based machine learning approach that relies on simple bitwise operations and finite-state automata, which makes it attractive for edge AI deployments. Recent work has focused on co-processor and accelerator designs based on Tsetlin Machines (TMs). Although these designs achieve high performance, they typically depend on tightly coupled interfaces, microcode-style programming, and external host processors, limiting flexibility and ease of programming. In this work, we present a domain-specific RISC-V microprocessor architecture and design flow tailored for TM inference. Leveraging the modular structure of RISC-V, we design a reduced instruction subset processor that retains programmability while targeting improved performance and lower energy consumption for TM workloads. Instruction profiling is employed to guide instruction reduction, followed by datapath and control path simplifications tailored to TM inference. Method: 提出 Kolmogorov-Arnold 储层计算（KARC），利用 Kolmogorov-Arnold 表示定理，以显式基函数展开替代传统的递归储层结构。该方法利用 KAN 的表达能力，同时通过闭式解实现高效训练。

Abstract: Reservoir computing offers a lightweight framework for forecasting dynamical systems but may struggle to capture long-range dependencies due to limited representational capacity. Conventional reservoir computing recurrently uses trainable reservoirs with hyperparameter sensitivity, while the next-generation reservoir computing removes recurrence at the cost of rapidly growing feature dimensions. Here, we develop Kolmogorov-Arnold Reservoir Computing (KARC), which replaces reservoirs with explicit basis-function expansions inspired by the Kolmogorov-Arnold representation theorem. We rigorously show that KARC is a lightweight design of Kolmogorov-Arnold networks (KANs), preserving the potential expressive capacity of KANs while admitting efficient closed-form training of reservoir computing. At comparable cost, KARC outperforms existing reservoir computing methods on challenging benchmarks including partial differential equations. It can also be integrated with generative diffusion models for text-to-image generation. This work thus establishes a principled bridge between reservoir computing and KANs, enabling efficient and high-fidelity dynamical system forecasting.

### [201] [Connect the Dots: Training LLMs for Long-Lifecycle Agents with Cross-Domain Generalization Via Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20002)
*Yanxi Chen,Weijie Shi,Yuexiang Xie,Boyi Hu,Yaliang Li,Bolin Ding,Jingren Zhou*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种名为“Connect the Dots”（CoD）的通用训练框架，核心包括：1. 结合任务求解与上下文更新的长序列端到端强化学习算法（采用GRPO风格及细粒度信用分配）；2. 专门设计的、旨在激发和评估LLM元能力的任务与环境体系，而非传统的单任务RL。

Abstract: This work presents a general framework for training large language models (LLMs) to "Connect the Dots" (CoD), a meta-capability required by long-lifecycle agents: as an LLM-based AI agent gets deployed in an environment, it solves a long sequence of tasks while continuously exploring the environment, learning from its own experiences, and iteratively self-updating its context about the environment, thereby achieving progressively better performance on future tasks conditioned on the updated context. Major components of the CoD framework include: (1) algorithm design and infrastructure for end-to-end reinforcement learning (RL) with long rollout sequences interleaving solve-task and update-context episodes; (2) tasks and environments for incentivizing and eliciting the targeted meta-capability in LLMs during training, as well as for faithfully measuring progress during evaluation. We present proof-of-concept implementations of the CoD framework, including a GRPO-style RL algorithm with fine-grained credit assignment, as well as tasks and environments tailored to the targeted meta-capability (rather than domain-specific LLM capabilities or standard task-by-task RL). Empirical results validate the efficacy of end-to-end RL training in the CoD setting, and demonstrate the potential for out-of-distribution generalization -- within the training domains, across different domains, and from CoD to Ralph-loop settings -- of the elicited meta-capability. Our investigation of CoD connects several lines of prior works, and opens up new opportunities for advancing LLMs and AI agents. To facilitate further research and applications, we release our implementations at \url{https://github.com/agentscope-ai/Trinity-RFT/tree/research/cod/examples/research_cod}.

### [202] [Activation- and Influence-Aware Ranks (AIR): Function-Preserving SVD Compression for LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19993)
*Nico Harder,Daniel Becking,Karsten Mueller,Wojciech Samek*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: AIR 是一种创新的 LLM 压缩框架，它通过引入反向信号影响力来优化 SVD 低秩分解，在大幅减少模型参数的同时，显著提升了模型性能并降低了计算开销，且能与现有技术兼容。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于 SVD 的大语言模型（LLM）压缩方法在处理参数缩减时，往往难以平衡模型精度与计算资源（如 FLOPs、内存占用、延迟）的权衡。作者旨在通过结合激活和反向传播影响力信息，进一步提升压缩后模型的性能。

Method: AIR 框架采用了基于 SVD（奇异值分解）的低秩近似方法，其核心创新在于：1. 引入了“影响力感知”度量，利用反向传播信号引导矩阵分解；2. 在 SVD-LLM(W) 的基础上，通过单次闭式交替最小二乘法（ALS）进行优化，并保证单调递减性质。

Result: 在参数保留率低于 60% 时，AIR 将困惑度（Perplexity）较 SVD-LLM(W) 提升超过 18%；在仅使用约 10% 的校准数据下即可达到同等质量；并有效实现了 FLOPs、内存和推理延迟的降低。

Conclusion: AIR 提供了一种高效的 LLM 模型压缩方案，能够通过引入反向传播信号的影响力感知，显著提升低秩分解的压缩质量，并可与其它压缩技术（如 LoRA）正交结合。

Abstract: We present Activation- and Influence-Aware Ranks (AIR), an SVD-based LLM compression framework that guides each weight matrix's low-rank approximation with a backward-signal influence metric. Starting from the activation-aware optimum of SVD-LLM(W), AIR runs a single closed-form alternating least squares (ALS) sweep that integrates influence element-wise under a monotone-descent guarantee. AIR is layer-local and composes orthogonally with end-to-end methods: alone it exceeds ACIP, and AIR+LoRA outperforms it further. AIR improves perplexity over SVD-LLM(W) by >18% at <=60% parameter retention, matches its quality with ~90% less calibration data, and turns parameter savings into FLOP, peak-memory, and per-token latency gains.

</details>


### [203] [What Makes Effective Supervision in Latent Chain-of-Thought: An Information-Theoretic Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20075)
*Xinghao Chen,Chak Tou Leong,Wenjin Guo,Jian Wang,Wenjie Li,Xiaoyu Shen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文从信息论角度揭示了隐式思维链（Latent CoT）训练中的双重坍缩问题，提出通过轨迹监督与生成式空间监督来维持推理过程的信息保真度，并验证了推理准确率与隐空间互信息之间的正相关性，为提升模型隐式推理能力提供了新范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的隐式思维链（Latent CoT）虽然通过隐藏状态进行推理，但仅依赖结果监督导致学习信号微弱，容易出现语义漂移，且推理过程难以控制，缺乏有效的监督机制。

Method: 1. 从信息论视角分析隐式思维链（Latent CoT），识别出梯度衰减与表征漂移的“双重坍缩”问题。
2. 将过程监督分解为“轨迹监督”（Trajectory Supervision）和“空间监督”（Space Supervision）。
3. 提出一种评估方法：统一隐式探针（Unified Latent Probe, ULP），用于量化隐式轨迹与显式推理步骤之间的互信息。
4. 实验对比了刚性几何压缩与生成式重构在维持语义结构方面的效果。

Result: 1. 证实了存在“信息-性能绑定”现象，即推理准确率与隐式链中保留的信息量呈正相关。
2. 证明了生成式重构比刚性几何压缩更能有效锚定语义空间，防止推理能力坍缩。
3. ULP 探针成功量化了隐式推理轨迹的信息保真度，为优化隐式推理提供了量化指标。

Conclusion: 研究表明，隐式思维链的性能与隐空间中保留的信息保真度（信息-性能绑定）直接相关。通过引入生成式重构作为语义锚点，而非强制的几何压缩，可以有效缓解训练中的双重坍缩，为开发更稳健、可解释的隐式推理模型提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Latent Chain-of-Thought (CoT) internalizes reasoning within continuous hidden states, offering a promising alternative to verbose discrete reasoning traces. However, robust latent reasoning remains difficult because outcome supervision provides weak learning signals and leaves latent trajectories prone to semantic drift. In this work, we analyze Latent CoT from an information-theoretic perspective and identify this failure as a dual collapse: gradient attenuation along the optimization path and representational drift in the latent space. We further decompose process supervision into two complementary dimensions: Trajectory Supervision, which injects dense stepwise reasoning signals, and Space Supervision, which preserves the semantic structure of the latent manifold. Our analysis shows that rigid geometric compression can collapse the reasoning space, whereas generative reconstruction provides a more flexible semantic anchor that better preserves information capacity. To measure these effects, we introduce the Unified Latent Probe (ULP), which quantifies the mutual information between latent trajectories and explicit reasoning steps. Experiments reveal a clear Information-Performance Binding: reasoning accuracy depends on the information fidelity preserved in the latent chain. These findings provide a principled framework for latent reasoning supervision and suggest shifting from geometric imitation toward mutual information maximization. Our code is available at \href{https://github.com/EIT-NLP/Supervision-in-Latent-CoT}{this repository}.

</details>


### [204] [StreamKL: Fast and Memory-Efficient KL Divergence for Boosting Attention Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20005)
*Guangda Liu,Yiquan Wang,Chengwei Li,Wenhao Chen,Jing Lin,Yiwu Yao,Danning Ke,Wenchao Ding,Jieru Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: StreamKL 是一种创新的 GPU 算子，它通过在线计算流式处理注意力分布，消除了长上下文蒸馏中的二次方显存需求，大幅提升了计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的注意力蒸馏方法在计算 KL 散度时，需要预先完整物化（Materialize）两个注意力分布矩阵，导致空间复杂度和 I/O 开销高达 O(NQN K)。这在处理长上下文（Long Context）任务时会产生严重的显存瓶颈，限制了模型蒸馏的扩展性。

Method: 提出了一种名为 StreamKL 的新型 GPU 融合算子。该方法通过在线计算公式推导，避免了注意力分布矩阵的显式存储（即去物化），采用单次遍历的核函数（Kernel）处理 Tile 块，并通过重计算（Recomputation）策略处理反向传播，从而将额外显存开销从 O(NQN K) 降低至 O(1)。

Result: 实验表明，StreamKL 在前向和反向传播中分别实现了最高 43 倍和 14 倍的加速，并将额外显存占用降至常数级别，使得在单张 GPU 上进行长上下文蒸馏成为可能。

Conclusion: StreamKL 通过数学重构实现了注意力蒸馏中 KL 散度计算的内存优化，从根本上解决了长上下文场景下的显存瓶颈，为高效的大模型训练与蒸馏提供了重要的底层支撑。

Abstract: Attention distillation, which trains one attention distribution to match another by minimizing their Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence, is widely used in knowledge distillation, model compression, continual learning, and sparse-attention LLM training. However, existing approaches materialize both attention distributions before computing the KL reduction, incurring $O(N_QN_K)$ memory and IO costs that become prohibitive at long context lengths. We present StreamKL, the first fused GPU primitive for attention KL divergence that eliminates this quadratic materialization. StreamKL derives a novel online formulation for the coupled two-distribution KL reduction, enabling a single one-pass forward kernel that streams query-key tiles through on-chip SRAM. For the backward pass, StreamKL recomputes attention probabilities tile-by-tile, avoiding storage of quadratic intermediates. We further design and implement efficient GPU kernels with dedicated optimizations. Experiments show StreamKL delivers up to $43\times$ and $14\times$ speedups over baseline methods in the forward and backward passes, respectively. Most importantly, StreamKL reduces the extra HBM footprint of attention distillation from $O(N_QN_K)$ to $O(1)$, enabling long-context distillation on a single GPU.

### [205] [VIMPO: Value-Implicit Policy Optimization for LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20008)
*Zhewei Kang,Aosong Feng,Sergey Levine,Dawn Song,Xuandong Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: VIMPO 是一种创新的无 Critic 策略优化方法，通过推导策略隐含的价值函数，实现了在不牺牲训练简单性的前提下，为大语言模型的推理任务提供更精准的信用分配，显著提升了模型在数学推理任务中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大语言模型的强化学习训练中，现有的方法存在权衡：GRPO 等组相对方法简单但信用分配不够细致（通常对所有 Token 分配相同的轨迹级优势）；而传统的 Actor-Critic 方法虽然能提供更密集的学习信号，但 Critic 的引入增加了训练的不稳定性。研究旨在寻找一种既能保留简单性又具备细粒度信用分配能力的优化方法。

Method: VIMPO（Value-Implied Policy Optimization）方法。该方法无需训练 Critic，而是通过 KL 正则化强化学习的最优性条件，推导出由策略隐含的价值函数（Policy-implied value function）。它利用自回归生成中的递归特性，将价值损失与最终的验证性奖励挂钩，并通过策略-参考对数比（Policy-reference log-ratios）进行锚定，实现了在保持架构简单的同时进行更精准的信用分配。

Result: 在 MATH-500、AIME 2024、AIME 2025 和 OlympiadBench 等数学验证性强化学习（RLVR）基准测试中，VIMPO 的表现均优于 GRPO，特别是在竞争级难度的评估中提升显著。此外，在噪声奖励环境下，VIMPO 依然保持了明显的优势，显示出其鲁棒性。

Conclusion: VIMPO 证明了通过 KL 正则化强化学习的最优性条件，可以在无需显式训练 Critic 的前提下，实现比传统组相对方法（如 GRPO）更细粒度的信用分配。这为大规模语言模型的推理能力提升提供了一种既高效又稳定的新路径。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards has become a central tool for improving the reasoning ability of large language models, but current methods face a trade-off between simplicity and credit assignment. Group-relative methods such as GRPO avoid training a critic, but typically assign a trajectory-level advantage to every token. Actor-critic methods provide denser learning signals, but require a learned value function with its own training instability. We introduce VIMPO, a critic-free policy optimization method that derives a policy-implied value function from the optimality conditions of KL-regularized reinforcement learning. For autoregressive generation, the resulting value recurrence can be written in terms of policy-reference log-ratios and anchored by the terminal condition that no future reward remains at the end of a trajectory. This gives a simple value loss that incorporates outcome-level verifiable rewards without training a critic. The same derivation also yields a critic-free actor advantage, allowing VIMPO to separate reward incorporation through the value loss from policy improvement through a PPO-style actor update. On mathematical RLVR benchmarks, VIMPO improves over GRPO across MATH-500, AIME 2024, AIME 2025, and OlympiadBench, with especially larger gains on competition-style evaluations. Under noisy rewards, VIMPO retains a consistent advantage over GRPO, suggesting that policy-implied value optimization can provide finer credit assignment while preserving the practical simplicity of critic-free training.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实工业场景（如金融销售数据）中存在显著的时间序列尺度异构性，而现有的全局归一化或窗口式缩放方法会导致低尺度信号压缩或语义信息丢失及反向缩放误差放大，亟需一种能兼顾语义判别性与数值精度的处理方法。

Method: 本文提出了一种自适应缩放（AS）模块，主要包含两个核心部分：1. 尺度校准（SC），利用神经网络学习并修正先验均值缩放因子；2. 缩放选择（SS），通过策略机制决定是否应用校准或保留原始尺度，从而在保持语义判别性的同时防止过度校准。

Result: 在蚂蚁财富和支付宝的真实基金销售数据集上的实验表明，AS模块能够无缝集成到主流时间序列预测模型中，并在多种评估指标上显著提升预测性能。

Conclusion: 本文提出的自适应缩放（AS）模块通过结合尺度校准和选择机制，有效解决了时间序列预测中因数据尺度异构性导致的性能下降问题，为多序列联合建模提供了鲁棒且高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Current time series forecasting (TSF) research predominantly focuses on scale-homogeneous data, where different time series share similar numerical magnitude ranges. However, in real-world industrial scenarios such as financial product sales, different time series often differ by orders of magnitude (scale heterogeneity). Since these series share similar temporal patterns, joint modeling is desirable for better data utilization, yet existing scaling methods either compress low-scale signals (global normalization) or destroy semantic discriminability and amplify inverse-scaling errors (window-based scaling). This paper proposes a self-Adaptive Scale-handling (AS) module that learns adaptive scale factors tailored to each input, preserving semantic discriminability while reducing inverse-scaling errors. AS consists of Scale Calibrating (SC), which calibrates prior mean scaling factors through neural networks, and Scaling Selection (SS), which decides whether to apply calibration or retain the original factor, avoiding over-calibration. Experiments on real-world fund sales datasets from Ant Fortune and Alipay show that AS seamlessly integrates into popular TSF models and consistently improves their performance. The code and dataset are available at the link https://github.com/Meteor-Stars/ASTSF.

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) has achieved strong performance in sequential decision-making, yet scaling to complex multi-agent environments remains challenging due to sparse rewards, large state-action spaces, and the difficulty of learning coordinated strategies. *Bilal Ahmed,Diab W. Abueidda,Waleed El-Sekelly,Tarek Abdoun,Mostafa E. Mobasher*

Abstract: Long-span roadway bridges exhibit highly localized structural responses under vehicular loading, making repeated FE analysis computationally expensive for applications such as influence surface generation and structural digital twins. Existing SciML approaches struggle to accurately capture these localized responses. To address this challenge, this study proposes an adaptive-trunk DeepONet for localized structural response prediction in large-scale bridge systems. The framework dynamically constructs a load-dependent learning domain using a KNN strategy, allowing the network to focus on structural influence zones. The trunk network is further enhanced using distance-aware features that encode the geometric relationship between the load and structural nodes. A physics-based full-field reconstruction is incorporated through a stiffness-informed Schur complement formulation, enabling predictions at adaptive nodes to be extended to the entire structural domain. To enable scalable training, response data are generated using a reduced-order equivalent shell model that preserves the dominant global behavior while significantly reducing computational cost. The proposed framework is validated on both a benchmark bridge model and the real-world Mussafah Bridge. Results show that the method achieves FEM-level accuracy with relative errors below 5%, while reducing the total response evaluation time (including full-field reconstruction) by approximately 60x; excluding the post-processing reconstruction step, the AD-DeepONet inference is up to four orders of magnitude faster than FEM. In addition, the framework enables rapid generation of full-field responses, influence lines, and influence surfaces under arbitrary vehicular loading configurations, demonstrating strong potential for large-scale bridge analysis and digital twin applications.

### [209] [Exploring the potential of AlphaEarth and TESSERA embeddings for Fine-scale Local Climate Zone Mapping: A case study across five cities in Switzerland](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20034)
*Htet Yamin Ko Ko,Clement Atzberger*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究利用TESSERA和AlphaEarth的预计算嵌入，对比传统的Sentinel-1/2复合影像，通过注意力机制的U-Net架构将低分辨率（100米）LCZ地图提升至10米分辨率。通过三个实验评估了跨城市可迁移性、高分辨率参考数据的影响以及模型对年度物候变化的鲁棒性。

Result: 实验表明，基于嵌入的模型在测试集上的IoU达到0.59-0.82；其中TESSERA表现最佳，优于S1S2和AlphaEarth。研究同时指出，跨年度模型的迁移仍然存在挑战，但嵌入方法能有效优化工作流程并提升制图的稳健性。

Conclusion: 利用地球观测基础模型（EO foundation models）生成的嵌入（embeddings）结合注意力U-Net架构，能够显著简化城市形态制图的预处理工作，提升LCZ制图的尺度、可迁移性与可重复性。未来提升精度的核心在于改善参考数据的质量。

Abstract: Understanding urban spatial morphology is critical for climate modeling, risk assessment, and sustainable urban design, and Local Climate Zone (LCZ) mapping provides the basic framework for this. However, many cities still use coarse ~100-m resolution LCZ records, which are unsuitable for fine-scale urban research. In this study, precomputed embeddings from TESSERA (Feng et al., 2025) and AlphaEarth (Brown et al., 2025) are compared to traditional Sentinel-1/2 (S1S2) composites in five Swiss cities to see if they can upscale coarse LCZ maps to 10-m resolution using an attention-based U-Net. Three experiments assess multi-city transferability, the impact of higher-resolution reference data, and temporal robustness to year-to-year phenology changes. We find that all datasets achieve strong performance with test data Intersection-over-Union (IoU) ranging from 0.59-0.69 and 0.77-0.82 in the first two experiments. TESSERA consistently outperforms both S1S2 and AlphaEarth across both settings As expected, we find that the transfer of embedding-based models from one year to another remains an open challenge. Overall, however, our results demonstrate the promising potential of embeddings derived from EO foundation models to reduce time consuming preprocessing, respectively, manual feature engineering tasks and to guide a universal deep learning-based LCZ mapping workflow. When combined with a simple location-aware attention U-Net architecture, the embeddings enhance regional transferability and scalability, supporting the development of comprehensive and reproducible fine-scale LCZ maps for global urban climate applications Improving reference data quality remains the strongest lever for further accuracy gains.

</details>


### [210] [Alzheimer's Disease Diagnosis using a Multimodal Approach with 3D MRI and PET](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20037)
*Loukas Ilias,Anthi-Maria Vozinaki,Christos Ntanos,Dimitris Askounis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种利用MRI和PET影像进行阿尔茨海默病诊断的输入自适应多模态学习模型。通过引入专家混合模型（MoE）实现动态特征路由，在提升诊断准确性的同时优化了计算效率，并通过Grad-CAM实现了模型的可解释性分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阿尔茨海默病（AD）的早期诊断对于延缓病情进展至关重要。现有的多模态影像（MRI和PET）融合方法通常采用静态连接方式，且对所有受试者执行相同的计算逻辑，这限制了模型对患者或数据源异质性的鲁棒性，且存在计算资源浪费。因此，作者旨在开发一种更灵活、高效且具备可解释性的多模态诊断模型。
